Unlike commercial drone detection, military UAV identification requires handling specialized reconnaissance platforms, loitering munitions, and tactical drones designed for stealth and operational effectiveness.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe system employs \u003cstrong\u003eYOLO11n (You Only Look Once v11)\u003c/strong\u003e, fine-tuned on a fully synthetic dataset containing 14 distinct military drone types. The synthetic training approach ensures perfect annotation accuracy while covering a diverse range of UAV configurations, from small tactical drones to larger MALE (Medium Altitude Long Endurance) platforms.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eDetected UAV Types\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Real-Time Military Drone Detection with YOLO11</h1><a id="user-content-real-time-military-drone-detection-with-yolo11" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Real-Time Military Drone Detection with YOLO11" href="#real-time-military-drone-detection-with-yolo11"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/16470bdb382cb91eb2b2c872248bcd35f117e4fea2f86ae024b125cf43d820fb/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f507974686f6e2d332e31312532422d626c75652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/16470bdb382cb91eb2b2c872248bcd35f117e4fea2f86ae024b125cf43d820fb/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f507974686f6e2d332e31312532422d626c75652e737667" alt="Python" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Python-3.11%2B-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/af5c3974d0d4ba25158f41797e9cd50dccc0d8b0b549718b4ef50a4029467e2b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f53747265616d6c69742d312e35302e302d6f72616e67652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/af5c3974d0d4ba25158f41797e9cd50dccc0d8b0b549718b4ef50a4029467e2b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f53747265616d6c69742d312e35302e302d6f72616e67652e737667" alt="Streamlit" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Streamlit-1.50.0-orange.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a85fbc79b86ded9cb69b60c4334d744b0bf8707ffe5ca35d9e257b0c62adf2f6/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f5079546f7263682d322e382532422d7265642e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a85fbc79b86ded9cb69b60c4334d744b0bf8707ffe5ca35d9e257b0c62adf2f6/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f5079546f7263682d322e382532422d7265642e737667" alt="PyTorch" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/PyTorch-2.8%2B-red.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b3cdc4a4efc966ad7478f3aa692eb0580057bce9e604f850cd8fe28560b0854c/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f594f4c4f31312d556c7472616c79746963732d626c75652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b3cdc4a4efc966ad7478f3aa692eb0580057bce9e604f850cd8fe28560b0854c/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f594f4c4f31312d556c7472616c79746963732d626c75652e737667" alt="Ultralytics" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/YOLO11-Ultralytics-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3dbeb98e052a14faa73bd25a37e6c512c22ec61dea147046d8ae58ddb5f4ec75/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4f70656e43562d342e31322d626c75652e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3dbeb98e052a14faa73bd25a37e6c512c22ec61dea147046d8ae58ddb5f4ec75/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4f70656e43562d342e31322d626c75652e737667" alt="OpenCV" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/OpenCV-4.12-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">A specialized detection system for identifying military unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) using the latest YOLO11 architecture. Trained on a synthetic dataset featuring combat drones including Shahed-136, Lancet, Orlan-10, and other reconnaissance and loitering munition platforms.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Idea: Military UAV Detection</h2><a id="user-content-core-idea-military-uav-detection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Idea: Military UAV Detection" href="#core-idea-military-uav-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This project addresses a critical defense technology challenge: <strong>automated detection of military drones in aerial surveillance systems</strong>. Unlike commercial drone detection, military UAV identification requires handling specialized reconnaissance platforms, loitering munitions, and tactical drones designed for stealth and operational effectiveness.</p>
<p dir="auto">The system employs <strong>YOLO11n (You Only Look Once v11)</strong>, fine-tuned on a fully synthetic dataset containing 14 distinct military drone types. The synthetic training approach ensures perfect annotation accuracy while covering a diverse range of UAV configurations, from small tactical drones to larger MALE (Medium Altitude Long Endurance) platforms.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Detected UAV Types</h2><a id="user-content-detected-uav-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Detected UAV Types" href="#detected-uav-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The model is trained to identify the following military drone platforms:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Shahed-131 / Shahed-136</strong> (Iranian loitering munitions - "Geran" in Russian service)</li>
<li><strong>Lancet</strong> (Russian loitering munition)</li>
<li><strong>Orlan-10</strong> (Russian reconnaissance UAV)</li>
<li><strong>ZALA 421-16E / ZALA 421-04M</strong> (Russian tactical reconnaissance)</li>
<li><strong>Forpost</strong> (Russian MALE UAV)</li>
<li><strong>Mohajer</strong> (Iranian reconnaissance platform)</li>
<li><strong>Granat-1 / Granat-2 / Granat-4</strong> (Russian tactical UAV series)</li>
<li><strong>SuperCam</strong> (Russian reconnaissance UAV)</li>
<li><strong>Techyon</strong> (Commercial/tactical platform)</li>
<li><strong>DJI Mavic 3</strong> (Commercial drone, military-adapted)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features</h2><a id="user-content-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features" href="#features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Specialized Military UAV Detection:</strong> Fine-tuned specifically for combat and reconnaissance drone platforms, not consumer quadcopters</li>
<li><strong>Synthetic Dataset Training:</strong> Trained on perfectly annotated synthetic data generated with Blender, ensuring zero labeling errors</li>
<li><strong>Real-Time Performance:</strong> Optimized for rapid detection with inference speeds suitable for operational deployment</li>
<li><strong>Multi-Modal Interface:</strong> Three detection modes - static image analysis, video processing, and live webcam surveillance</li>
<li><strong>Comprehensive Web Interface:</strong> Streamlit-based application for easy deployment and testing</li>
<li><strong>Production-Ready Pipeline:</strong> Complete workflow from dataset preparation through training to deployment</li>
<li><strong>Adjustable Sensitivity:</strong> Configurable confidence thresholds to balance detection rate vs. false alarm rate</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting Started</h2><a id="user-content-getting-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting Started" href="#getting-started"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This project requires Python 3.11+ and uses <code>uv</code> for fast dependency management.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Clone the repository</h3><a id="user-content-1-clone-the-repository" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Install <code>uv</code> (if you don't have it)</h3><a id="user-content-2-install-uv-if-you-dont-have-it" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Install uv (if you don't have it)" href="#2-install-uv-if-you-dont-have-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Create environment and install dependencies</h3><a id="user-content-3-create-environment-and-install-dependencies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Create environment and install dependencies" href="#3-create-environment-and-install-dependencies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Create the virtual environment
uv venv

# Activate the environment
# For Windows (PowerShell):
.\.venv\Scripts\activate
# For MacOS/Linux (bash/zsh):
source .venv/bin/activate

# Install all required packages
uv pip install ultralytics opencv-python streamlit pillow"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create the virtual environment</span>
uv venv

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Activate the environment</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For Windows (PowerShell):</span>
.<span class="pl-cce">\.</span>venv<span class="pl-cce">\S</span>cripts<span class="pl-cce">\a</span>ctivate
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For MacOS/Linux (bash/zsh):</span>
<span class="pl-c1">source</span> .venv/bin/activate

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install all required packages</span>
uv pip install ultralytics opencv-python streamlit pillow</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Download the dataset</h3><a id="user-content-4-download-the-dataset" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Download the dataset" href="#4-download-the-dataset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Download the military drones dataset from Kaggle:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Dataset:</strong> <a href="https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/banderastepan/drone-detection" rel="nofollow">banderastepan/drone-detection</a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Option 1: Using Kaggle API
uv pip install kaggle
kaggle datasets download -d banderastepan/drone-detection

uv pip install kaggle
kaggle datasets download -d banderastepan/drone-detection
unzip drone-detection.zip -d drone-detection

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Train the model</h3><a id="user-content-5-train-the-model" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Train the model" href="#5-train-the-model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python main.py"><pre>python main.py</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will automatically:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Prepare the dataset (split into train/val/test)</li>
<li>Train YOLO11n for 100 epochs (~30-60 minutes on GPU)</li>
<li>Validate the model performance</li>
<li>Save the trained model to <code>results/military_drone_model/weights/best.pt</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. <p dir="auto">The user interface provides:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Image Upload:</strong> Drag-and-drop support for JPG, JPEG, and PNG formats</li>
<li><strong>Video Processing:</strong> Upload MP4, AVI, or MOV files for frame-by-frame detection</li>
<li><strong>Confidence Control:</strong> Dynamic threshold adjustment (0.0-1.0) for detection sensitivity</li>
<li><strong>Real-Time Camera:</strong> Live webcam integration for continuous surveillance</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technical Implementation</h2><a id="user-content-technical-implementation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technical Implementation" href="#technical-implementation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Architecture Overview</h3><a id="user-content-architecture-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Architecture Overview" href="#architecture-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The detection pipeline implements:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Dataset Preparation</strong> → Synthetic dataset organization with train/val/test splits (80/15/5)</li>
<li><strong>Data Loading</strong> → YOLO format parsing with automatic verification</li>
<li><strong>Model Training</strong> → YOLO11n fine-tuning with specialized augmentation strategy</li>
<li><strong>Inference Engine</strong> → GPU-accelerated detection with configurable confidence filtering</li>
<li><strong>Post-Processing</strong> → Non-maximum suppression and bounding box extraction</li>
<li><strong>Visualization</strong> → OpenCV-based annotation rendering</li>
<li><strong>Web Interface</strong> → Streamlit multi-modal interaction layer</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Technologies</h3><a id="user-content-key-technologies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Technologies" href="#key-technologies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>YOLO11n Model:</strong> Nano variant optimized for speed-accuracy balance (2.58M parameters, 6.3 GFLOPs)</li>
<li><strong>Synthetic Training Data:</strong> Blender-generated imagery with perfect annotations</li>
<li><strong>Streamlit Framework:</strong> Rapid prototyping framework for ML model deployment</li>
<li><strong>OpenCV (cv2):</strong> Video I/O, frame processing, and visualization</li>
<li><strong>PyTorch Backend:</strong> Deep learning framework powering YOLO11</li>
<li><strong>640x640 Resolution:</strong> Standardized image size matching dataset specifications</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Training Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-training-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Training Configuration" href="#training-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Optimized parameters for military UAV detection:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="model.train(
    epochs=100,             # Extended training for accuracy
    imgsz=640,              # Matches dataset resolution
    batch=16,               # Optimized for 8GB VRAM
    device=0,               # CUDA GPU acceleration

    # Augmentation strategy
    hsv_h=0.015,           # Minimal hue shift
    hsv_s=0.7,             # Strong saturation variance
    hsv_v=0.5,             # Brightness (day/night simulation)
    degrees=10,            # Slight rotation (banking drones)
    scale=0.7,             # Multi-scale for distance variance
    flipud=0.0,            # No vertical flip
    fliplr=0.5,            # Horizontal flip enabled
    mosaic=1.0,            # Mosaic augmentation
    mixup=0.1,             # Mixup for robustness

    # Optimization
    optimizer='auto',       # Automatic selection
    lr0=0.01,              # Initial learning rate
    warmup_epochs=3,       # Warmup period
    amp=True,              # Mixed precision training
)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">model</span>.<span class="pl-c1">train</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">epochs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>,             <span class="pl-c"># Extended training for accuracy</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">imgsz</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">640</span>,              <span class="pl-c"># Matches dataset resolution</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">batch</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">16</span>,               <span class="pl-c"># Optimized for 8GB VRAM</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,               <span class="pl-c"># CUDA GPU acceleration</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># Augmentation strategy</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">hsv_h</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.015</span>,           <span class="pl-c"># Minimal hue shift</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">hsv_s</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.7</span>,             <span class="pl-c"># Strong saturation variance</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">hsv_v</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>,             <span class="pl-c"># Brightness (day/night simulation)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">degrees</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>,            <span class="pl-c"># Slight rotation (banking drones)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">scale</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.7</span>,             <span class="pl-c"># Multi-scale for distance variance</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">flipud</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.0</span>,            <span class="pl-c"># No vertical flip</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">fliplr</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>,            <span class="pl-c"># Horizontal flip enabled</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">mosaic</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>,            <span class="pl-c"># Mosaic augmentation</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">mixup</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.1</span>,             <span class="pl-c"># Mixup for robustness</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># Optimization</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'auto'</span>,       <span class="pl-c"># Automatic selection</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">lr0</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.01</span>,              <span class="pl-c"># Initial learning rate</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">warmup_epochs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">3</span>,       <span class="pl-c"># Warmup period</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">amp</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>,              <span class="pl-c"># Mixed precision training</span>
)</pre></div>
<hr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dataset Details</h2><a id="user-content-dataset-details" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dataset Details" href="#dataset-details"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Source:</strong> Kaggle - banderastepan/drone-detection</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Characteristics:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Type:</strong> Fully synthetic (Blender-generated)</li>
<li><strong>Resolution:</strong> 640x640 pixels (standardized)</li>
<li><strong>Annotations:</strong> YOLO format (<code>class_id center_x center_y width height</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Accuracy:</strong> 100% annotation accuracy (synthetic generation)</li>
<li><strong>Classes:</strong> Single class ("drone") covering 14 military UAV types</li>
<li><strong>Coverage:</strong> Iranian, Russian, and commercial platforms</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Advantages of Synthetic Data:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Perfect label accuracy (no human annotation errors)</li>
<li>Controlled lighting and environmental conditions</li>
<li>Diverse viewing angles and distances</li>
<li>No operational security concerns</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configuration" href="#configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Model Selection</h3><a id="user-content-model-selection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Model Selection" href="#model-selection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Switch to larger YOLO variants for improved accuracy (in <code>main.py</code>):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="model = YOLO('yolo11s.pt')  # Small: better accuracy, slower
model = YOLO('yolo11m.pt')  # Medium: balanced
model = YOLO('yolo11l.pt')  # Large: high accuracy
model = YOLO('yolo11x.pt')  # Extra large: maximum accuracy"><pre><span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">YOLO</span>(<span class="pl-s">'yolo11s.pt'</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># Small: better accuracy, slower</span>
<span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">YOLO</span>(<span class="pl-s">'yolo11m.pt'</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># Medium: balanced</span>
<span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">YOLO</span>(<span class="pl-s">'yolo11l.pt'</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># Large: high accuracy</span>
<span class="pl-s1">model</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">YOLO</span>(<span class="pl-s">'yolo11x.pt'</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># Extra large: maximum accuracy</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Training Duration</h3><a id="user-content-training-duration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Training Duration" href="#training-duration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Adjust epochs for convergence:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="epochs=100  # Default: good balance

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Detection Threshold</h3><a id="user-content-detection-threshold" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Detection Threshold" href="#detection-threshold"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Modify confidence in <code>app.py</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="confidence = st.sidebar.slider(&quot;Confidence&quot;, 0.1, 0.9, 0.25)
# Lower: more detections, higher false alarm rate
# Higher: fewer detections, lower false alarm rate"><pre><span class="pl-s1">confidence</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">st</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sidebar</span>.<span class="pl-c1">slider</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Confidence"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.1</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.9</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.25</span>)
<span class="pl-c"># Lower: more detections, higher false alarm rate</span>
<span class="pl-c"># Higher: fewer detections, lower false alarm rate</span></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Interpretation:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>95.6% Precision:</strong> When model detects a drone, it's correct 95.6% of the time (low false alarm rate)</li>
<li><strong>90.7% Recall:</strong> Successfully detects 9 out of 10 drones present in imagery</li>
<li><strong>2.7ms Inference:</strong> Capable of ~370 FPS processing speed on NVIDIA RTX 4060</li>
<li><strong>Confidence threshold 0.40</strong> recommended to eliminate false positives from birds and other aerial objects</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Learning Outcomes</h2><a id="user-content-learning-outcomes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Learning Outcomes" href="#learning-outcomes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This project demonstrates advanced capabilities in:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ Training specialized object detection models for defense applications</li>
<li>✅ Working with synthetic training data and understanding its advantages</li>
<li>✅ Implementing domain-specific augmentation strategies</li>
<li>✅ Building production ML pipelines from data preparation to deployment</li>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Troubleshooting</h2><a id="user-content-troubleshooting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Troubleshooting" href="#troubleshooting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dataset not found</h3><a id="user-content-dataset-not-found" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dataset not found" href="#dataset-not-found"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ensure you've downloaded and extracted the Kaggle dataset:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="ls drone-detection/  # Should show images/ and labels/"><pre>ls drone-detection/  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Should show images/ and labels/</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CUDA out of memory</h3><a id="user-content-cuda-out-of-memory" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CUDA out of memory" href="#cuda-out-of-memory"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Reduce batch size in <code>main.py</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="batch=8  # or batch=4 for 4GB VRAM"><pre><span class="pl-s1">batch</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">8</span>  <span class="pl-c"># or batch=4 for 4GB VRAM</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Low performance metrics</h3><a id="user-content-low-performance-metrics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Low performance metrics" href="#low-performance-metrics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Increase training epochs to 150+</li>
<li>Try larger model variant (yolo11s or yolo11m)</li>
<li>Verify dataset quality with <code>python inspect_dataset.py</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Slow inference</h3><a id="user-content-slow-inference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Slow inference" href="#slow-inference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ensure GPU is being used (check CUDA availability)</li>
<li>Export model to ONNX or TensorRT for deployment</li>
<li>Consider using smaller input size (imgsz=416)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Future Enhancements</h2><a id="user-content-future-enhancements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Future Enhancements" href="#future-enhancements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Incomplete task"> Integration with counter-UAS systems</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Operational Considerations</h2><a id="user-content-operational-considerations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Operational Considerations" href="#operational-considerations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Disclaimer:</strong> This is an educational/research project demonstrating computer vision techniques. Deployment in operational defense systems requires:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Validation on real-world imagery (not synthetic data alone)</li>
<li>Integration with existing command &amp; control systems</li>
<li>Extensive field testing in various environmental conditions</li>
<li>Compliance with relevant regulations and protocols</li>
<li>Redundancy and failsafe mechanisms</li>
<li>Regular model updates as new UAV types emerge</li>
</ul>
